This aggressive pricing strategy aligns with our growth-focused objective and aims to attract more consumers, thus increasing our market share.  
EXPECTED: I expect to increase our market share to approximately 15% this round, leading to a profit impact of around $1,500,000, assuming our volume of loans increases significantly due to the lower rate.
```

#### Decision Summary:

- **Reasoning:** By setting the interest rate at 450 bps, I am positioning B08 competitively below the average market rate of 500 bps while still maintaining a margin above our cost of funds (280 bps) and operating costs.
